# <a name="obsolete-types-in-the-net-framework"></a><span data-ttu-id="929d2-102">Tipi obsoleti in .NET Framework</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="929d2-102">Obsolete Types in the .NET Framework</span></span>
<a name="introduction"></a> <span data-ttu-id="929d2-103">Le tabelle in questo articolo elencano i tipi obsoleti in [!INCLUDE[net_v45](../../../includes/net-v45-md.md)] e [!INCLUDE[net_v46](../../../includes/net-v46-md.md)], organizzati per assembly.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="929d2-103">The tables in this article list the types that are obsolete in the [!INCLUDE[net_v45](../../../includes/net-v45-md.md)] and the [!INCLUDE[net_v46](../../../includes/net-v46-md.md)], organized by assembly.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="929d2-104">Usare i seguenti collegamenti per vedere un elenco di tipi obsoleti e le alternative consigliate in ogni assembly.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="929d2-104">Use the following links to see a list of the obsolete types and the recommended alternatives in each assembly.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="929d2-105">Poiché questi tipi sono obsoleti, lo sono anche tutti i relativi membri.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="929d2-105">Because these types are obsolete, all their members are also obsolete.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="929d2-106">Per un elenco di altri membri obsoleti nella libreria di classi .NET Framework, vedere [Membri obsoleti](../../../docs/framework/whats-new/obsolete-members.md).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="929d2-106">For a list of additional obsolete members in the .NET Framework class library, see [Obsolete Members](../../../docs/framework/whats-new/obsolete-members.md).</span></span>

 <span data-ttu-id="929d2-134">Nelle seguenti tabelle sono elencati i tipi dichiarati obsoleti negli assembly di sistema.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="929d2-134">The following tables list the types that have been declared obsolete in system assemblies.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="929d2-135">Questi assembly vengono usati per lo sviluppo di applicazioni generiche destinate a .NET Framework.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="929d2-135">These assemblies are used for general\-purpose application development that targets the .NET Framework.</span></span>

<a name="obsolete_types_in_microsoft_assemblies"></a>
## <a name="obsolete-types-in-microsoft-assemblies"></a><span data-ttu-id="929d2-925">Tipi obsoleti negli assembly Microsoft</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="929d2-925">Obsolete Types in Microsoft Assemblies</span></span>
 <span data-ttu-id="929d2-926">Nelle seguenti sezioni sono elencati i tipi obsoleti contenuti negli assembly Microsoft.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="929d2-926">The following sections list the obsolete types in Microsoft assemblies.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="929d2-927">Questi ultimi sono assembly speciali, ad esempio assembly destinati a un unico linguaggio (es. Microsoft.JScript.dll o Microsoft.VisualC.dll).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="929d2-927">These assemblies are special-purpose assemblies such as assemblies that target an individual language (for example, Microsoft.JScript.dll or Microsoft.VisualC.dll).</span></span>

<a name="IEHost"></a>
